# Word list for a specific language.
# In this file, line starts with # (comments) and empty lines are ignored
# Word list is organize like this :	
# $GRAMMAR$ : describe how extract word and frequency from following list. 
# The grammar affect following lines, this way its possible to have several grammar in the file. 
# When a new grammar is found, it replace the actual grammar for the rest of list, until meet an other $GRAMMAR$ (or reach end of document)

# Default $GRAMMAR$ definition : 
$GRAMMAR$	<frequency>[SPACE]<word>
# Where :
# 		<frequency> is the place for the integer for frequency
# 		[SPACE] one or more "space characters" (Space, tabulation)
# 		<word> is the place for the "word"

# *****************************************
# ***   French word initial word list   ***
# *****************************************
